# <a name="required-mobile-diagnostic-data-for-microsoft-teams"></a><span data-ttu-id="8663b-103">Dados de diagnóstico móvel necessários para o Microsoft Teams</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-103">Required mobile diagnostic data for Microsoft Teams</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="8663b-104">O artigo a seguir contém uma lista de eventos do Microsoft Teams para dispositivos móveis e listas de propriedades que cada evento coleta.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-104">The following article contains a list of Microsoft Teams mobile events, and lists of properties each event collects.</span></span>

## <a name="events"></a><span data-ttu-id="8663b-105">Eventos</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-105">Events</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="8663b-106">Existem propriedades comuns para todos os eventos listados abaixo, para revisá-los, consulte [Propriedades enviadas com todos os eventos](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-106">There are common properties for all events listed below, to review them, see [Properties sent with all events](#properties-sent-with-all-events).</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="8663b-1472">Scenario_StatusCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-1472">Scenario_StatusCode</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="8663b-1473">A propriedade registra o código do status com base no sucesso ou na falha do cenário</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="8663b-1473">Property records status code of the scenario based on scenario success or failure</span></span> |
